    5571            0 : void jit_avx512_core_amx_bwd_weights_kernel_t::balance(const jit_conv_conf_t &j,

    5589              :         /* calculate per thread memory cost (read/write). high level optimizer
    5590              :          * tries to minimize memory consumption. few notes:
    5591              :          *  (n1) if weights tensor size is less than source and destination
    5592              :          *       tensors we apply the ratio of the source and destination
    5593              :          *       tensor sizes to weights one as compensation coefficient to
    5594              :          *       avoid parallelization across batch size only, othervise we
    5595              :          *       apply additional coefficient to source component based on
    5596              :          *       performance measurements
    5597              :          *  (n2) use scales based on output vs input channels ratio for source
    5598              :          *       and destination componets to imporve threading balance across
    5599              :          *       input and output channels */
    5600              : 
    5601            0 :         const dim_t src_type_size = 2;
    5602            0 :         const dim_t wei_type_size = 4;
    5603              : 
    5604            0 :         dim_t src_size
    5605            0 :                 = (dim_t)j.mb * j.ic * j.id * j.ih * j.tr_iw * src_type_size;
    5606            0 :         dim_t dst_size
    5607            0 :                 = (dim_t)j.mb * j.oc * j.od * j.oh * j.tr_ow * src_type_size;
    5608            0 :         dim_t wei_size
    5609            0 :                 = (dim_t)j.oc * j.ic * j.kd * j.kh * j.kw * wei_type_size;
    5610              : 
    5611            0 :         float wei_compensation_scale = 0.5f * (dst_size + src_size) / wei_size;
    5612            0 :         float oi_channels_ratio = (float)(j.nb_oc / j.nb_oc_blocking)
    5613            0 :                 / (j.nb_ic / j.nb_ic_blocking);
    5614            0 :         auto get_src_coef = [oi_channels_ratio, wei_compensation_scale]() {
    5615            0 :             float src_coef = nstl::max(1.0f / oi_channels_ratio, 1.0f);
    5616            0 :             if (wei_compensation_scale < 1.0f) src_coef *= 4.0f;
    5617              : 
    5618            0 :             return src_coef;
    5619            0 :         };
    5620              : 
    5621            0 :         auto get_dst_coef = [oi_channels_ratio]() {
    5622            0 :             return nstl::max(oi_channels_ratio, 1.0f);
    5623            0 :         };
    5624              : 
    5625            0 :         auto get_wei_coef = [wei_compensation_scale]() {
